##### **Null Space Constrained Contrastive Visual Forgetting for MLLM Unlearning**
2605.05909v1 by Yuhang Wang, Zhenxing Niu, Haoxuan Ji, Guangyu He, Linlin Zhang, Haichang Gao

The core challenge of machine unlearning is to strike a balance between target knowledge removal and non-target knowledge retention. In the context of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs), this challenge becomes even more pronounced, as knowledge is further divided into visual and textual modalities that are tightly intertwined. In this paper, we introduce an MLLM unlearning approach that aims to forget target visual knowledge while preserving non-target visual knowledge and all textual knowledge. Specifically, we freeze the LLM backbone and achieve unlearning by fine-tuning the visual module. First, we propose a Contrastive Visual Forgetting (CVF) mechanism to separate target visual knowledge from retained visual knowledge, guiding the representations of target visual concepts toward appropriate regions in the feature space. Second, we identify the null space associated with retained knowledge and constrain the unlearning process within this space, thereby significantly mitigating degradation in knowledge retention. Third, beyond static unlearning scenarios, we extend our approach to continual unlearning, where forgetting requests arrive sequentially. Extensive experiments across diverse benchmarks demonstrate that our approach achieves a strong balance between effective forgetting and robust knowledge retention.

摘要：機器遺忘的核心挑戰在於在目標知識移除與非目標知識保留之間取得平衡。在多模態大型語言模型（MLLMs）的背景下，這一挑戰變得更加明顯，因為知識進一步分為緊密交織的視覺和文本模態。在本文中，我們介紹了一種 MLLM 遺忘方法，旨在忘記目標視覺知識，同時保留非目標視覺知識和所有文本知識。具體而言，我們凍結 LLM 骨幹，並通過微調視覺模塊來實現遺忘。首先，我們提出了一種對比視覺遺忘（CVF）機制，以將目標視覺知識與保留的視覺知識分開，指導目標視覺概念的表示朝向特徵空間中的適當區域。其次，我們識別與保留知識相關的零空間，並將遺忘過程限制在這個空間內，從而顯著減輕知識保留的退化。第三，除了靜態遺忘場景外，我們將我們的方法擴展到持續遺忘，其中遺忘請求依次到達。對各種基準的廣泛實驗表明，我們的方法在有效遺忘和穩健知識保留之間達到了良好的平衡。

##### **CITE: Anytime-Valid Statistical Inference in LLM Self-Consistency**
2605.05873v1 by Hirofumi Ota, Naoto Iwase, Yuki Ichihara, Junpei Komiyama, Masaaki Imaizumi

Large language models often improve reasoning by sampling multiple outputs and aggregating their final answers, but precise and efficient control of error levels remains a challenging task. In particular, deciding when to stop sampling remains difficult when the stopping rule is data-dependent and the set of possible answers is not known in advance. We study anytime-valid certification of a prespecified target answer as the unique mode of the model's response distribution, a guarantee distinct from answer correctness. We propose the Certification by Intersection-union Testing with E-processes (CITE) algorithm, which provably controls false certification at any prescribed level under arbitrary data-driven stopping, without requiring prior knowledge of the answer category set. We also prove an category-set-size-free stopping-time rate, establish matching minimax lower bounds up to constants in the main regime, and extend the construction to confidence-weighted voting. Simulations and LLM self-consistency experiments show empirical error control and improved certification in diffuse-tail settings.

摘要：大型語言模型通常透過取樣多個輸出並聚合最終答案來改善推理，但精確且高效地控制錯誤水平仍然是一項具有挑戰性的任務。<lb/>特別是，當停止規則依賴於數據且可能的答案集事先未知時，決定何時停止取樣仍然困難。<lb/>我們研究了對預先指定的目標答案進行隨時有效的認證，作為模型回應分佈的唯一模式，這是一種與答案正確性不同的保證。<lb/>我們提出了交集-聯合測試的認證算法（CITE），該算法在任意數據驅動的停止情況下，能夠在任何規定的水平下可證明地控制虛假認證，而不需要事先知道答案類別集。<lb/>我們還證明了一個不依賴於類別集大小的停止時間率，建立了在主要範疇中與常數匹配的最小最大下界，並將該構造擴展到信心加權投票。<lb/>模擬和大型語言模型自我一致性實驗顯示了在擴散尾部設置中的經驗錯誤控制和改進的認證。

##### **XDecomposer: Learning Prior-Free Set Decomposition for Multiphase X-ray Diffraction**
2605.05866v1 by Hanyu Gao, Bin Cao, Yunyue Su, Tong-Yi Zhang, Qiang Liu

Multiphase powder X-ray diffraction (PXRD) analysis remains a fundamental bottleneck in structure identification, as real-world synthesis often produces complex mixtures whose constituent phases (components) cannot be reliably disentangled. While recent advances in representation-based crystal retrieval and generation suggest the possibility of inferring structures directly from PXRD, existing approaches largely assume single-phase inputs and break down in multiphase settings. Here, we present XDecomposer, a prior-free framework for joint decomposition and identification of multiphase XRD patterns without requiring candidate phase lists, structural templates, or prior knowledge of phase number. We formulate multiphase diffraction analysis as a set prediction problem, where the model infers an unordered set of phase-resolved components, their mixture proportions, and corresponding structural representations within a unified architecture. A phase-query-driven decomposition mechanism, together with diffraction-consistent physical reconstruction, enables accurate source separation while preserving crystallographic fidelity. Extensive experiments on both simulated and experimental datasets show that XDecomposer substantially improves reconstruction accuracy and phase identification across diverse chemical systems, while maintaining strong generalization to unseen mixtures. These results provide a practical route toward data-driven, source-resolved multiphase XRD analysis and reduce long-standing dependence on prior-guided iteratively phase matching. The code is openly available at https://github.com/Licht0812/XDecomposer

摘要：多相粉末 X 射線衍射 (PXRD) 分析仍然是結構識別中的一個基本瓶頸，因為現實世界的合成通常產生複雜的混合物，其組成相 (成分) 無法可靠地分離。雖然最近在基於表示的晶體檢索和生成方面的進展暗示了直接從 PXRD 推斷結構的可能性，但現有的方法大多假設單相輸入，並在多相環境中失效。在這裡，我們提出了 XDecomposer，一個無需先驗的框架，用於多相 XRD 圖案的聯合分解和識別，而不需要候選相列表、結構模板或相數的先驗知識。我們將多相衍射分析公式化為一個集合預測問題，其中模型推斷一組無序的相解析組件、它們的混合比例以及在統一架構內的相應結構表示。一個基於相查詢的分解機制，加上與衍射一致的物理重建，使得準確的源分離成為可能，同時保持晶體學的保真度。在模擬和實驗數據集上的大量實驗顯示，XDecomposer 顯著提高了重建精度和相識別能力，涵蓋了多種化學系統，同時對未見混合物保持了強大的泛化能力。這些結果提供了一條實用的途徑，朝向數據驅動的、源解析的多相 XRD 分析，並減少了對先驗引導的迭代相匹配的長期依賴。代碼可在 https://github.com/Licht0812/XDecomposer 獲得。

##### **SOPE: Stabilizing Off-Policy Evaluation for Online RL with Prior Data**
2605.05863v1 by Carlo Romeo, Girolamo Macaluso, Alessandro Sestini, Andrew D. Bagdanov

Incorporating prior data into online reinforcement learning accelerates training but typically forces a difficult trade-off between high computational costs and long, multi-stage training pipelines. While fixed-length stabilization phases are significantly more computationally efficient than static update schedules, they require task-dependent manual tuning, risking either the waste of prior knowledge or severe overfitting. To address this, we propose SOPE, an algorithm that uses an actor-aligned Off-Policy Policy Evaluation (OPE) signal as an automated early-stopping mechanism to dynamically control the length of offline training phases. By evaluating the critic on a held-out validation split under the current policy's action distribution, SOPE halts gradient updates exactly when out-of-distribution benefits saturate, eliminating the need for manual schedule tuning. Evaluated on 25 continuous control tasks from the Minari benchmark suite, SOPE improves baseline performance by up to 45.6% while reducing the required TFLOPs by up to 22x, thus balancing the tradeoff between sample and computational efficiency. These findings demonstrate that adaptive, evaluation-driven update schedules are more effective than relying on static, exhaustive update schedules.

摘要：將先前的數據納入在線增強學習可以加速訓練，但通常會迫使在高計算成本和長期、多階段訓練流程之間做出困難的權衡。雖然固定長度的穩定階段在計算效率上顯著高於靜態更新計劃，但它們需要依賴任務的手動調整，這可能導致先前知識的浪費或嚴重的過擬合。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了SOPE，一種使用與演員對齊的離線策略評估（OPE）信號作為自動早停機制的算法，以動態控制離線訓練階段的長度。通過在當前策略的行動分佈下對保留的驗證數據集評估評論者，SOPE在出現分佈外的效益飽和時精確停止梯度更新，消除了手動調整計劃的需要。在Minari基準套件中的25個連續控制任務上進行評估，SOPE將基準性能提高了最高45.6%，同時將所需的TFLOPs減少了最高22倍，從而平衡了樣本和計算效率之間的權衡。這些發現表明，基於評估驅動的自適應更新計劃比依賴靜態的、全面的更新計劃更有效。

##### **LeakDojo: Decoding the Leakage Threats of RAG Systems**
2605.05818v1 by Maosen Zhang, Jianshuo Dong, Boting Lu, Wenyue Li, Xiaoping Zhang, Tianwei Zhang, Han Qiu

Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) enables large language models (LLMs) to leverage external knowledge, but also exposes valuable RAG databases to leakage attacks. As RAG systems grow more complex and LLMs exhibit stronger instruction-following capabilities, existing studies fall short of systematically assessing RAG leakage risks. We present LeakDojo, a configurable framework for controlled evaluation of RAG leakage. Using LeakDojo, we benchmark six existing attacks across fourteen LLMs, four datasets, and diverse RAG systems. Our study reveals that (1) query generation and adversarial instructions contribute independently to leakage, with overall leakage well approximated by their product; (2) stronger instruction-following capability correlates with higher leakage risk; and (3) improvements in RAG faithfulness can introduce increased leakage risk. These findings provide actionable insights for understanding and mitigating RAG leakage in practice. Our codebase is available at https://github.com/yeasen-z/LeakDojo.

摘要：檢索增強生成（RAG）使大型語言模型（LLMs）能夠利用外部知識，但也使得有價值的RAG數據庫面臨洩漏攻擊的風險。隨著RAG系統變得越來越複雜，LLMs展現出更強的指令遵循能力，現有研究未能系統性地評估RAG洩漏風險。我們提出了LeakDojo，一個可配置的框架，用於控制評估RAG洩漏。使用LeakDojo，我們在十四個LLMs、四個數據集和多樣的RAG系統中基準測試了六種現有攻擊。我們的研究揭示了：（1）查詢生成和對抗性指令獨立地對洩漏做出貢獻，整體洩漏可通過它們的乘積良好近似；（2）更強的指令遵循能力與更高的洩漏風險相關；以及（3）RAG忠實度的改善可能引入更高的洩漏風險。這些發現為理解和減輕實際中的RAG洩漏提供了可行的見解。我們的代碼庫可在 https://github.com/yeasen-z/LeakDojo 獲得。

##### **Sheet as Token: A Graph-Enhanced Representation for Multi-Sheet Spreadsheet Understanding**
2605.05811v1 by Yiming Lei, Yiqi Wang, Yujia Zhang, Bo Guan, Depei Zhu, Chunhui Wang, Zhuonan Hao, Tianyu Shi

Workbook-scale spreadsheet understanding is increasingly important for language-model-based data analysis agents, but remains challenging because relevant information is often distributed across multiple sheets with heterogeneous schemas, layouts, and implicit relationships. Existing retrieval-augmented approaches typically decompose spreadsheets into rows, columns, or blocks to improve scalability; however, such chunk-centric representations can fragment worksheets into isolated text spans and weaken global sheet-level semantics. We propose Sheet as Token, a graph-enhanced framework that treats each worksheet as a unified semantic unit for multi-sheet spreadsheet retrieval. Our method extracts schema-aware records from sheet names, column headers, representative values, and layout features, and encodes each worksheet into a compact dense token. Given a natural-language query, a Graph Retriever constructs a query-specific candidate graph over sheet tokens using semantic, query-conditioned, schema-consistency, and shape-compatibility relations, and composes these channels through a multi-stage graph transformer to retrieve supporting sheet sets. Experiments on a constructed multi-sheet spreadsheet corpus show that sheet-level tokenization learns stable representations, and that graph-enhanced cross-sheet reasoning improves listwise retrieval over a shallow graph baseline with limited additional graph-side computation. These results suggest that sheet-level tokenization is a promising abstraction for scalable multi-sheet spreadsheet understanding.

摘要：工作簿規模的電子表格理解對於基於語言模型的數據分析代理越來越重要，但仍然具有挑戰性，因為相關信息通常分佈在多個具有異質架構、佈局和隱含關係的工作表中。現有的檢索增強方法通常將電子表格分解為行、列或區塊以提高可擴展性；然而，這種以塊為中心的表示可能會將工作表碎片化為孤立的文本片段，並削弱全局工作表級別的語義。我們提出了“工作表作為標記”（Sheet as Token），這是一個增強圖形的框架，將每個工作表視為多工作表電子表格檢索的統一語義單元。我們的方法從工作表名稱、列標題、代表性值和佈局特徵中提取具備架構意識的記錄，並將每個工作表編碼為一個緊湊的密集標記。給定自然語言查詢，圖形檢索器基於語義、查詢條件、架構一致性和形狀兼容性關係，構建一個查詢特定的候選圖形，並通過多階段圖形變換器組合這些通道以檢索支持的工作表集。對構建的多工作表電子表格語料庫的實驗表明，工作表級別的標記化學習穩定的表示，並且增強圖形的跨工作表推理在有限的額外圖形側計算下改善了基於淺圖形基線的列表檢索。這些結果表明，工作表級別的標記化是一種有前景的抽象，適用於可擴展的多工作表電子表格理解。

##### **LCC-LLM: Leveraging Code-Centric Large Language Models for Malware Attribution**
2605.05807v1 by Christopher G. Pedraza Pohlenz, Hassan Jalil Hadi, Ali Hassan, Ali Shoker

LLMs are increasingly explored for malware analysis; however, current LLM-based malware attribution remains limited by unsupported indicators and insufficient code-level grounding for identifying malicious and vulnerable code segments. To address these limitations, this research introduces LCC-LLM, a code-centric benchmark dataset and evidence-grounded framework for malware attribution and multi-task static malware analysis. The proposed LCCD dataset contains approximately 34K PE samples processed through a large-scale reverse-engineering pipeline and represented using decompiled C code, assembly code, CFG/FCG artifacts, hexadecimal data, PE metadata, suspicious API evidence, and structural features. Beyond dataset construction, LCC-LLM integrates LangGraph-orchestrated static analysis with multi-source cybersecurity knowledge to support evidence-grounded malware reasoning. The framework employs a seven-layer retrieval-augmented generation pipeline, CoVe for IoC validation, and a multi-dimensional quality gate to improve factual reliability and analyst-oriented decision support. Curriculum-ordered instruction data is used to fine-tune DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-14B and Qwen3-Coder-30B-A3B using QLoRA. Evaluation across 43 malware-analysis task types achieves an average semantic similarity of 0.634, with the highest task-level performance in structured report generation, IoC extraction, vulnerability assessment, malware configuration extraction, and malware class detection. In a real-world case study using MalwareBazaar samples, the grounded pipeline achieves a 10/10 structured analysis pass rate, producing CFG/FCG evidence, MITRE ATT&CK mappings, detection guidance, and analyst-ready reports. These results show that code-centric representations, retrieval grounding, and verification-guided reasoning improve the reliability and operational usefulness of LLM-assisted malware attribution.

##### **CircuitFormer: A Circuit Language Model for Analog Topology Design from Natural Language Prompt**
2605.05773v1 by Md Touhidul Islam, Sujan Kumar Saha, Farimah Farahmandi, Mark Tehranipoor

Automating analog circuit design remains a longstanding challenge in Electronic Design Automation (EDA). While Transformer-based Large Language Models (LLMs) have revolutionized software code generation, their application to analog hardware design is hindered by two critical limitations: (i) the scarcity of analog design datasets containing natural language description of a design and its corresponding netlist, and (ii) the inefficiency of general-purpose tokenizers (e.g., Byte Pair Encoding (BPE)) in capturing the inherent graph structure of circuits. To bridge this gap, first, we curate the largest annotated dataset of analog circuit netlists to date, comprising 31,341 netlist-natural language description pairs across all major circuit classes. Furthermore, we propose Circuit Tokenizer (CKT), a novel circuit graph tokenizer designed to encode netlist connectivity by explicitly mining frequent subcircuits. In terms of scalability, CKT overcomes the bottleneck of prior circuit graph serialization methods where vocabulary size scales linearly with maximum number of components in the dataset, n_max, (O(n_max)); instead, CKT decouples vocabulary growth from circuit complexity, achieving a constant O(1) complexity. Empirically, CKT outperforms standard BPE on circuit topology representation, reducing sequence length by 57% and achieving a 2.3x superior compression ratio using a compact, fixed vocabulary of size 512. Leveraging this optimized tokenization, we train a circuit-specific language model, CircuitFormer, a 511M parameter encoder-decoder transformer. Our model achieves 100% syntactic correctness and an 83% functional success rate across all major analog circuit categories, outperforming state-of-the-art open-source LLMs by 10% and 14%, respectively, while requiring 240x fewer parameters. The dataset is publicly available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/touhid314/cktformer-dataset.

摘要：自動化類比電路設計仍然是電子設計自動化（EDA）中的一項長期挑戰。雖然基於Transformer的大型語言模型（LLMs）已經徹底改變了軟體代碼生成，但它們在類比硬體設計中的應用受到兩個關鍵限制的阻礙：（i）缺乏包含設計自然語言描述及其對應網路清單的類比設計數據集，以及（ii）通用分詞器（例如，字節對編碼（BPE））在捕捉電路固有圖結構方面的低效。為了填補這一空白，我們首先整理了迄今為止最大的類比電路網路清單註釋數據集，涵蓋了所有主要電路類別中的31,341對網路清單-自然語言描述。此外，我們提出了Circuit Tokenizer（CKT），這是一種新穎的電路圖分詞器，旨在通過明確挖掘頻繁的子電路來編碼網路清單的連通性。在可擴展性方面，CKT克服了先前電路圖序列化方法的瓶頸，這些方法的詞彙大小隨著數據集中最大元件數量n_max（O(n_max)）線性增長；相反，CKT將詞彙增長與電路複雜性解耦，實現了恆定的O(1)複雜度。在實證上，CKT在電路拓撲表示上超越了標準BPE，將序列長度減少了57%，並使用大小為512的緊湊固定詞彙達到了2.3倍的優越壓縮比。利用這種優化的分詞，我們訓練了一個電路特定的語言模型CircuitFormer，一個511M參數的編碼器-解碼器Transformer。我們的模型在所有主要類比電路類別中達到了100%的語法正確性和83%的功能成功率，分別超越了最先進的開源LLMs 10%和14%，同時需要的參數少了240倍。該數據集可在https://huggingface.co/datasets/touhid314/cktformer-dataset公開獲取。

##### **CoMemNet: Contrastive Sampling with Memory Replay Network for Continual Traffic Prediction**
2605.05738v1 by Mei Wu, Wenchao Weng, Wenxin Su, Wenjie Tang, Wei Zhou

In recent years, the integration of non-topological space modeling with temporal learning methods has emerged as an effective approach for capturing spatio-temporal information in non-Euclidean graphs. However, most existing methods rely on static underlying graph structures, which are inadequate for capturing the continuously expanding and evolving patterns in streaming traffic networks. To address this challenge, we propose a simple yet efficient dual-branch continual learning framework for traffic prediction, named CoMemNet. The fast-converging Online branch undertakes the primary prediction tasks, while the momentum-updated Target branch extracts historical information using Wasserstein Distance features to create a Dynamic Contrastive Sampler (DC Sampler). This sampler selects a node set with significant dynamic network feature changes for training, effectively mitigating the issue of catastrophic forgetting. Additionally, the backbone incorporates a lightweight Node-Adaptive Temporal Memory Buffer (TMRB-N) to consolidate old knowledge through memory replay and address the risk of memory explosion. Finally, we provide two newly curated open-source datasets. Experimental results demonstrate that CoMemNet achieves state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance across all three large-scale real-world datasets. The code is available at: https://github.com/meiwu5/CoMemNet.

摘要：近年來，非拓撲空間建模與時間學習方法的整合已成為捕捉非歐幾里得圖中時空信息的有效方法。<lb/>然而，大多數現有方法依賴於靜態的基礎圖結構，這對於捕捉流量網絡中不斷擴展和演變的模式來說是不足夠的。<lb/>為了解決這一挑戰，我們提出了一個簡單而高效的雙分支持續學習框架，用於流量預測，名為 CoMemNet。<lb/>快速收斂的在線分支承擔主要的預測任務，而動量更新的目標分支則利用 Wasserstein 距離特徵提取歷史信息，以創建動態對比取樣器（DC Sampler）。<lb/>這個取樣器選擇一組在動態網絡特徵變化上顯著的節點集進行訓練，有效地減輕了災難性遺忘的問題。<lb/>此外，主幹還包含一個輕量級的節點自適應時間記憶緩衝區（TMRB-N），通過記憶重播來鞏固舊知識，並解決記憶爆炸的風險。<lb/>最後，我們提供了兩個新編輯的開源數據集。<lb/>實驗結果表明，CoMemNet 在所有三個大型現實世界數據集中達到了最先進的（SOTA）性能。<lb/>代碼可在以下網址獲得：https://github.com/meiwu5/CoMemNet。

##### **Active Learning for Communication Structure Optimization in LLM-Based Multi-Agent Systems**
2605.05703v1 by Huchen Yang, Xinghao Dong, Dan Negrut, Jin-Long Wu

Optimizing the communication structure of large language model based multi-agent systems (LLM-MAS) has been shown to improve downstream performance and reduce token usage. Existing methods typically rely on randomly sampled training tasks. However, tasks may differ substantially in difficulty and domain, and thus they are not equally informative for updating communication structure, making optimization under limited training budgets often unstable and highly sensitive to the particular training set. To actively identify the most valuable tasks for communication-structure optimization, we propose an ensemble-based information-theoretic task selection framework. The proposed method estimates task informativeness by how much a candidate task changes the distribution over graph parameters, using ensemble Kalman inversion as an efficient and derivative-free approximation of the corresponding Bayesian update. The resulting estimator is especially suitable for black-box and noisy multi-agent systems. To enhance scalability, we construct a compact candidate pool through embedding-based representative selection and combine the informative selection with surrogate modeling and batch Thompson sampling. We validate our method in both benign settings and settings with agent attacks, demonstrating its effectiveness for communication-structure optimization under constrained computational budgets.

##### **Knowledge-Graph Paths as Intermediate Supervision for Self-Evolving Search Agents**
2605.05702v1 by Huyu Wu, Jun Liu, Xiaochi Wei, Yan Gao, Yi Wu, Yao Hu

Self-evolving search agents reduce reliance on human-written training questions by generating and solving their own search tasks. We build on Search Self-Play (SSP), a representative Proposer and Solver framework in which questions are generated and answered via multi-step search and reasoning. In practice, however, SSP faces two bottlenecks: the Proposer constructs questions from isolated answer entities without relational context, yielding many invalid or unverifiable questions in early self-play training, while the Solver receives only a binary outcome reward that discards useful signal from partially on-track search trajectories. We address both bottlenecks by reusing knowledge-graph paths as construction-derived intermediate supervision for both question construction and reward shaping. First, we ground question construction in LLM-guided knowledge-graph subgraphs, providing relational context for the Proposer. Second, we observe that constructing and solving a multi-hop question can involve overlapping intermediate entities: the factual bridges used to formulate the question may provide approximate waypoints for answering it. Exploiting this overlap, we introduce Waypoint Coverage Reward (WCR), which grants graded partial credit to incorrect Solver trajectories according to their coverage of entities on the construction path, while preserving full reward for correct answers. Across seven QA benchmarks and nine model configurations, our approach improves the average score over standard SSP in all configurations, including notable gains on multi-hop QA tasks. These results suggest that knowledge-graph paths can be reused as lightweight intermediate supervision, providing both relational guidance and process feedback without additional task-specific human annotations or manually labeled process steps.

摘要：自我演化的搜索代理減少了對人類編寫的訓練問題的依賴，通過生成和解決自己的搜索任務。我們基於搜索自我遊戲（SSP），這是一個具有代表性的提議者和解決者框架，其中問題通過多步搜索和推理生成和回答。然而，在實踐中，SSP面臨兩個瓶頸：提議者從孤立的答案實體構建問題，缺乏關聯上下文，導致在早期自我遊戲訓練中產生許多無效或不可驗證的問題，而解決者僅獲得二元結果獎勵，這丟棄了部分在軌搜索軌跡中的有用信號。我們通過重用知識圖譜路徑作為構建衍生的中間監督來解決這兩個瓶頸，適用於問題構建和獎勵塑造。首先，我們將問題構建基於LLM引導的知識圖譜子圖，為提議者提供關聯上下文。其次，我們觀察到構建和解決多跳問題可能涉及重疊的中間實體：用於形成問題的事實橋樑可能為回答問題提供近似的途徑點。利用這種重疊，我們引入了途徑點覆蓋獎勵（WCR），根據解決者在構建路徑上的實體覆蓋情況，對不正確的解決者軌跡給予分級部分信用，同時對正確答案保留全額獎勵。在七個QA基準和九個模型配置中，我們的方法在所有配置中提高了標準SSP的平均分數，包括在多跳QA任務上顯著的增益。這些結果表明，知識圖譜路徑可以作為輕量級中間監督重用，提供關聯指導和過程反饋，而無需額外的任務特定人類註釋或手動標記的過程步驟。

##### **GCCM: Enhancing Generative Graph Prediction via Contrastive Consistency Model**
2605.05689v1 by Shaozhen Ma, Wei Huang, Hanchen Wang, Dong Wen, Wenjie Zhang

Conditional generative models, particularly diffusion-based methods, have recently been applied to graph prediction by modeling the target as a conditional distribution given the input graph, yielding competitive results compared to deterministic predictor. However, existing diffusion-based prediction methods typically require expensive iterative denoising at inference and often suffer from unstable sampling, which motivates recent efforts to reduce inference denoising steps and enable stable sampling via techniques such as consistency training. Despite this progress, we find that existing consistency training methods for graph prediction could potentially fall into a shortcut solution: the model may attempt to satisfy the self-consistency constraint by ignoring the noisy target (i.e., assigning it negligible weight), ultimately collapsing into a purely deterministic predictor. To mitigate such shortcut solution, we propose GCCM, a graph contrastive consistency model that goes beyond isolated pairwise matching between the same target at different noise levels by introducing negative pairs into a contrastive consistency objective. This adds an additional separation requirement, making the shortcut solution no longer trivially sufficient to satisfy the proposed objective. Moreover, we apply feature perturbation to the input node/edge features to break identical conditioning on the input graph, so that the shortcut no longer yields the same predictions across noise levels and becomes less attractive. Extensive experiments on benchmark datasets demonstrate that GCCM mitigates the shortcut solution and yields consistent performance improvements in graph prediction compared to deterministic predictors.

摘要：條件生成模型，特別是基於擴散的方法，最近已被應用於圖形預測，通過將目標建模為給定輸入圖形的條件分佈，產生了與確定性預測器相比具有競爭力的結果。<lb/>然而，現有的基於擴散的預測方法通常在推斷時需要昂貴的迭代去噪，並且經常遭受不穩定的取樣，這促使最近的努力減少推斷去噪步驟並通過一致性訓練等技術實現穩定取樣。<lb/>儘管有這些進展，我們發現現有的圖形預測一致性訓練方法可能會陷入捷徑解決方案：模型可能試圖通過忽略噪聲目標（即，給予其微不足道的權重）來滿足自我一致性約束，最終崩潰為純粹的確定性預測器。<lb/>為了減輕這種捷徑解決方案，我們提出了GCCM，一種圖形對比一致性模型，它通過將負對進入對比一致性目標，超越了在不同噪聲水平下對同一目標的孤立成對匹配。<lb/>這增加了一個額外的分離要求，使得捷徑解決方案不再輕易滿足所提出的目標。<lb/>此外，我們對輸入節點/邊特徵應用特徵擾動，以打破對輸入圖形的相同條件，這樣捷徑不再在不同噪聲水平下產生相同的預測，變得不那麼有吸引力。<lb/>在基準數據集上的廣泛實驗表明，GCCM減輕了捷徑解決方案，並在圖形預測中相比確定性預測器產生了一致的性能提升。

##### **DataDignity: Training Data Attribution for Large Language Models**
2605.05687v1 by Xiaomin Li, Andrzej Banburski-Fahey, Jaron Lanier

Auditing language-model outputs often requires more than judging correctness: an auditor may need to identify which source document most likely supports the knowledge expressed in a response. We study this as pinpoint provenance: given a prompt, a target-model response, and a candidate corpus, rank the documents that best support the response. We introduce FakeWiki, a controlled benchmark of 3,537 fabricated Wikipedia-style articles designed to preserve ground-truth provenance while weakening lexical shortcuts. FakeWiki includes QA probes, source-preserving paraphrases, retro-generated variants, hard anti-documents that remain topically similar while removing answer-critical facts, and five query conditions: clean prompting plus four jailbreak-inspired transformations. We evaluate seven retrieval baselines, a training-free activation-steering retrieval-fusion method, SteerFuse, and a supervised contrastive provenance ranker, ScoringModel. ScoringModel maps response and document features into a shared space and is trained with InfoNCE using in-batch, retrieval-mined, and anti-document negatives. Across nine open-weight instruction-tuned LLMs and five query conditions, ScoringModel improves mean Recall@10 from 35.0 for the strongest retrieval baseline to 52.2, without inference-time fusion, and wins 41/45 model-by-condition cells. SteerFuse is usually second-best despite requiring no supervised training, showing that activation-space evidence can efficiently complement text retrieval. On jailbreak-inspired transformed queries, ScoringModel improves Recall@10 by 15.7 points on average over the best baseline. Overall, our work shows that robust training data attribution requires evaluation settings that separate true answer support from topical or lexical resemblance.

摘要：審計語言模型的輸出通常需要的不僅僅是判斷正確性：審計員可能需要識別哪個來源文件最有可能支持回應中表達的知識。我們將此研究稱為精確來源：給定一個提示、一個目標模型的回應和一個候選語料庫，對最能支持該回應的文件進行排名。我們引入了FakeWiki，一個包含3,537篇虛構維基百科風格文章的受控基準，旨在保留真實來源的同時削弱詞彙捷徑。FakeWiki包括問答探針、保留來源的改寫、逆向生成的變體、在主題上保持相似但移除關鍵事實的困難反文件，以及五種查詢條件：乾淨提示加上四種靈感來自越獄的轉換。我們評估了七個檢索基線、一種無需訓練的激活引導檢索融合方法SteerFuse，以及一個監督對比來源排名器ScoringModel。ScoringModel將回應和文件特徵映射到共享空間，並使用InfoNCE進行訓練，使用批內、檢索挖掘和反文件的負樣本。在九個開放權重指令調整的LLM和五種查詢條件下，ScoringModel將平均Recall@10從最強檢索基線的35.0提高到52.2，且無需推理時融合，並在41/45的模型與條件單元中獲勝。儘管SteerFuse不需要監督訓練，但通常是第二好的，顯示出激活空間證據可以有效補充文本檢索。在靈感來自越獄的轉換查詢中，ScoringModel的Recall@10平均提高了15.7個點，超過最佳基線。總體而言，我們的工作表明，穩健的訓練數據歸屬需要評估設置，將真實答案支持與主題或詞彙相似性分開。

##### **Attractor Geometry of Transformer Memory: From Conflict Arbitration to Confident Hallucination**
2605.05686v1 by Qiyao Liang, Risto Miikkulainen, Ila Fiete

Language models draw on two knowledge sources: facts baked into weights (parametric memory, PM) and information in context (working memory, WM). We study two mechanistically distinct failure modes--conflict, when PM and WM disagree and interfere; and hallucination, when the queried fact was never learned. Both produce confident output regardless, making output-based monitoring blind by design. We show both failures share a unified geometric account. In the hidden-state space of autoregressive generation, learned facts form attractor basins. Conflict is basin competition: WM disrupts convergence to the correct basin without raising output entropy. Hallucination is basin absence: the hidden state drifts freely when no memorized basin exists. The frozen LM head, designed for next-token prediction, cannot distinguish these cases and fires confidently either way. We verify this account in a controlled synthetic task--entity identifiers mapped to unique codes with PM installed via LoRA adapters--where ground truth is exact and component roles can be causally isolated through targeted adapter placement. Geometric margin--the hidden state's distance to the nearest memorized basin--reads this geometry directly and separates correct recall from hallucination far more cleanly than output entropy, with zero false refusals where entropy-based detection cannot avoid rejecting the vast majority of correct outputs. The separation holds on natural-language factual queries from the pretrained model with no adaptation, confirming attractor geometry is structural rather than a fine-tuning artifact. The fraction of confident hallucinations follows a scaling law $C = \exp(-c/\barΔ)$, growing with scale even as overall error rates fall. Hidden states reliably encode epistemic state; the frozen output head systematically erases it--and this erasure worsens with scale.

摘要：語言模型依賴兩種知識來源：內嵌於權重中的事實（參數記憶，PM）和上下文中的信息（工作記憶，WM）。我們研究兩種機制上不同的失效模式——衝突，當PM和WM不一致並相互干擾時；以及幻覺，當被查詢的事實從未學習過時。無論如何，這兩者都會產生自信的輸出，這使得基於輸出的監控在設計上是盲目的。我們展示這兩種失效共享一個統一的幾何解釋。在自回歸生成的隱藏狀態空間中，學習到的事實形成吸引子盆地。衝突是盆地競爭：WM在不提高輸出熵的情況下破壞了對正確盆地的收斂。幻覺是盆地缺失：當不存在任何記憶盆地時，隱藏狀態自由漂移。為下一個標記預測設計的凍結LM頭無法區分這些情況，並且無論如何都會自信地觸發。我們在一個受控的合成任務中驗證了這一解釋——實體標識符映射到唯一代碼，並通過LoRA適配器安裝PM——其中真實情況是精確的，並且組件角色可以通過有針對性的適配器放置進行因果隔離。幾何邊際——隱藏狀態到最近記憶盆地的距離——直接讀取這一幾何，並比輸出熵更清晰地區分正確回憶和幻覺，且在熵基檢測無法避免拒絕絕大多數正確輸出的情況下，零假拒絕。這種區分在未經調整的預訓練模型的自然語言事實查詢中保持不變，確認吸引子幾何是結構性的，而非微調的產物。自信幻覺的比例遵循一個縮放法則 $C = \exp(-c/\barΔ)$，隨著規模增長，即使整體錯誤率下降。隱藏狀態可靠地編碼認知狀態；凍結的輸出頭系統性地抹去了它——而這種抹去隨著規模的增長而惡化。

##### **Text-Graph Synergy: A Bidirectional Verification and Completion Framework for RAG**
2605.05643v1 by Jiarui Zhong, Hong Cai Chen

Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) has become a core paradigm for enhancing factual grounding and multi-hop reasoning in Large Language Models (LLMs). Traditional text-based RAG often retrieves logically irrelevant pseudo-evidence, while graph-based RAG is frequently hindered by search-time pruning, which may discard potentially valid reasoning paths. Existing hybrid approaches primarily adopt simple evidence concatenation or unidirectional enhancement, which fails to address the fundamental "Information Island" problem caused by asymmetric reasoning flows between unstructured text and structured graphs. We propose \textbf{TGS-RAG}, a unified framework for \textbf{T}ext-\textbf{G}raph \textbf{S}ynergistic enhancement. TGS-RAG introduces a bidirectional mechanism: (i) a \textbf{Graph-to-Text} channel that employs a Global Voting strategy from visited graph nodes to re-rank and refine textual evidence, filtering out semantic noise; and (ii) a \textbf{Text-to-Graph} channel that utilizes the \textbf{Memory-based Orphan Entity Bridging} algorithm. This algorithm utilizes textual cues to proactively resurrect valid but previously pruned reasoning paths from the search history without additional database overhead. Experimental results on multiple multi-hop reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that TGS-RAG significantly outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, achieving a superior balance between retrieval precision and computational efficiency.

摘要：檢索增強生成（RAG）已成為提升大型語言模型（LLMs）事實基礎和多跳推理的核心範式。傳統的基於文本的RAG經常檢索到邏輯上無關的偽證據，而基於圖的RAG則常常受到搜索時間修剪的阻礙，這可能會丟棄潛在有效的推理路徑。現有的混合方法主要採用簡單的證據串聯或單向增強，這無法解決由於非結構化文本和結構化圖之間不對稱推理流所引起的根本“信息孤島”問題。我們提出了\textbf{TGS-RAG}，一個統一的\textbf{T}ext-\textbf{G}raph \textbf{S}ynergistic增強框架。TGS-RAG引入了一個雙向機制：（i）一個\textbf{Graph-to-Text}通道，利用來自訪問過的圖節點的全局投票策略來重新排序和精煉文本證據，過濾掉語義噪音；（ii）一個\textbf{Text-to-Graph}通道，利用\textbf{基於記憶的孤立實體橋接}算法。該算法利用文本提示主動恢復有效但先前被修剪的推理路徑，無需額外的數據庫開銷。多個多跳推理基準的實驗結果表明，TGS-RAG顯著超越了最先進的基準，在檢索精度和計算效率之間達到了更好的平衡。

##### **Architecture Matters: Comparing RAG Systems under Knowledge Base Poisoning**
2605.05632v1 by Samuel Korn

Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems are vulnerable to knowledge base poisoning, yet existing attacks have been evaluated almost exclusively against vanilla retrieve-then-generate pipelines. Architectures designed to handle conflicting retrieved information - multi-agent debate, agentic retrieval, recursive language models - remain untested against adversarially optimized contradictions. We evaluate four RAG architectures (vanilla RAG, agentic RAG, MADAM-RAG, and Recursive Language Models) under controlled single-document (N=1) poisoning on 921 Natural Questions QA pairs, comparing a clean baseline, naive injection, and CorruptRAG-AK - an adversarial attack whose meta-epistemic framing targets credibility assessment. Architecture is a high-impact variable in adversarial robustness: under CorruptRAG-AK, attack success rates range from 81.9% (vanilla) to 24.4% (RLM) - a spread of nearly 58 percentage points across architectures with comparable clean accuracy (~92%). Decomposing this gap, once the poisoned document is retrieved, adversarial framing - not retrieval optimization - drives the majority of CorruptRAG-AK's advantage for three of four architectures, localizing the cross-architecture vulnerability at the content-reasoning stage. Our MADAM-RAG reimplementation shows the highest apparent contradiction detection rate, though our LLM judge over-identifies this behavior (~48.5% precision), so reported rates are upper bounds. Regardless of detection, MADAM-RAG cannot resolve contradictions reliably, producing a 41.4% non-answer rate even on clean inputs - though implementation divergences from the original may contribute. We introduce a seven-category behavioral taxonomy capturing contradiction detection, hedging, and failure modes beyond binary accuracy. Code, data, and analysis notebooks are publicly available.

摘要：檢索增強生成（RAG）系統易受到知識庫中毒的影響，但現有的攻擊幾乎僅針對原始的檢索-然後-生成管道進行評估。旨在處理衝突檢索信息的架構——多代理辯論、代理檢索、遞歸語言模型——尚未針對對抗性優化的矛盾進行測試。我們在921個自然問題問答對上，對四種RAG架構（原始RAG、代理RAG、MADAM-RAG和遞歸語言模型）進行了受控的單文檔（N=1）中毒評估，並比較了乾淨基線、天真注入和CorruptRAG-AK——一種對抗性攻擊，其元認識框架針對信譽評估。架構是對抗穩健性中的一個高影響變量：在CorruptRAG-AK下，攻擊成功率範圍從81.9%（原始）到24.4%（RLM）——在具有可比乾淨準確度（約92%）的架構中，差距近58個百分點。分解這一差距後，一旦檢索到中毒文檔，對抗性框架——而非檢索優化——驅動了CorruptRAG-AK在四種架構中三種的優勢，將跨架構的脆弱性定位在內容推理階段。我們的MADAM-RAG重新實現顯示出最高的明顯矛盾檢測率，儘管我們的LLM判斷者過度識別了這一行為（約48.5%的精確度），因此報告的比率是上限。無論檢測如何，MADAM-RAG無法可靠地解決矛盾，即使在乾淨輸入上也產生41.4%的無答案率——儘管與原始實現的差異可能會有所貢獻。我們引入了一個七類行為分類法，捕捉矛盾檢測、對沖和超越二元準確度的失敗模式。代碼、數據和分析筆記本公開可用。

##### **One Turn Too Late: Response-Aware Defense Against Hidden Malicious Intent in Multi-Turn Dialogue**
2605.05630v1 by Xinjie Shen, Rongzhe Wei, Peizhi Niu, Haoyu Wang, Ruihan Wu, Eli Chien, Bo Li, Pin-Yu Chen, Pan Li

Hidden malicious intent in multi-turn dialogue poses a growing threat to deployed large language models (LLMs). Rather than exposing a harmful objective in a single prompt, increasingly capable attackers can distribute their intent across multiple benign-looking turns. Recent studies show that even modern commercial models with advanced guardrails remain vulnerable to such attacks despite advances in safety alignment and external guardrails. In this work, we address this challenge by detecting the earliest turn at which delivering the candidate response would make the accumulated interaction sufficient to enable harmful action. This objective requires precise turn-level intervention that identifies the harm-enabling closure point while avoiding premature refusal of benign exploratory conversations. To further support training and evaluation, we construct the Multi-Turn Intent Dataset (MTID), which contains branching attack rollouts, matched benign hard negatives, and annotations of the earliest harm-enabling turns. We show that MTID helps enable a turn-level monitor TurnGate, which substantially outperforms existing baselines in harmful-intent detection while maintaining low over-refusal rates. TurnGate further generalizes across domains, attacker pipelines, and target models. Our code is available at https://github.com/Graph-COM/TurnGate.

摘要：隱藏的惡意意圖在多輪對話中對部署的大型語言模型（LLMs）構成日益增長的威脅。攻擊者不再在單一提示中暴露有害目標，而是可以在多個看似無害的回合中分散他們的意圖。最近的研究顯示，即使是具有先進防護措施的現代商業模型，仍然對這類攻擊保持脆弱，儘管在安全對齊和外部防護措施方面有所進展。在這項工作中，我們通過檢測在何時交付候選回應會使累積的互動足以啟用有害行為的最早回合來應對這一挑戰。這一目標需要精確的回合級干預，以識別使害處成為可能的結束點，同時避免過早拒絕無害的探索性對話。為了進一步支持訓練和評估，我們構建了多輪意圖數據集（MTID），該數據集包含分支攻擊展開、匹配的無害強負樣本以及最早使害處成為可能的回合的註釋。我們顯示MTID有助於啟用回合級監控器TurnGate，該監控器在有害意圖檢測中顯著超越現有基準，同時保持低拒絕率。TurnGate在不同領域、攻擊者管道和目標模型之間進一步泛化。我們的代碼可在 https://github.com/Graph-COM/TurnGate 獲得。

##### **Belief Memory: Agent Memory Under Partial Observability**
2605.05583v1 by Junfeng Liao, Qizhou Wang, Jianing Zhu, Bo Du, Rui Yan, Xiuying Chen

LLM agents that operate over long context depend on external memory to accumulate knowledge over time. However, existing methods typically store each observation as a single deterministic conclusion (e.g., inferring "API~X failed" from temporary errors), even though such observations are inherently partial and potentially ambiguous. By committing to one conclusion and discarding uncertainty, these methods introduce self-reinforcing error: the agent acts on the stored conclusion, never revisits alternatives, and reinforces the conclusion over time. To address this issue, we propose BeliefMem, which shifts the memory paradigm from committing to a single conclusion per observation to retaining multiple candidate conclusions with their probabilities. Concretely, BeliefMem stores the candidate conclusions as separate memory entries, each carrying a probability that is updated via Noisy-OR rules as new observations arrive. At retrieval, all candidates surface together with their probabilities, keeping alternatives visible to the agent. Since each conclusion in memory retains its probability, BeliefMem preserves the uncertainty that the deterministic paradigm discards, enabling the agent to act with high confidence on well-evidenced knowledge while retaining the capacity to update its confidence when new evidence arrives. Empirical evaluations on LoCoMo and ALFWorld benchmarks show that, even with limited data, BeliefMem achieves the best average performance, remarkably outperforming well-known baselines. More broadly, such probabilistic memory produces substantial gains and explores a new direction for agent memory in partially observable environments.

摘要：LLM 代理在長上下文中運作依賴外部記憶來隨時間累積知識。<lb/>然而，現有的方法通常將每個觀察存儲為單一的確定性結論（例如，從臨時錯誤推斷「API~X 失敗」），儘管這些觀察本質上是部分的且可能含糊不清。<lb/>通過承諾一個結論並丟棄不確定性，這些方法引入了自我強化的錯誤：代理根據存儲的結論行動，從不重新考慮其他選擇，並隨著時間的推移強化該結論。<lb/>為了解決這個問題，我們提出了 BeliefMem，這一方法將記憶範式從對每個觀察承諾單一結論轉變為保留多個候選結論及其概率。<lb/>具體而言，BeliefMem 將候選結論作為獨立的記憶條目存儲，每個條目攜帶一個隨著新觀察到來而通過 Noisy-OR 規則更新的概率。<lb/>在檢索時，所有候選結論及其概率一起顯現，使代理能夠看到替代選擇。<lb/>由於記憶中的每個結論保留其概率，BeliefMem 保留了確定性範式所丟棄的不確定性，使代理能夠在充分證據的知識上自信地行動，同時在新證據到來時保留更新其信心的能力。<lb/>在 LoCoMo 和 ALFWorld 基準上的實證評估顯示，即使在數據有限的情況下，BeliefMem 也達到了最佳的平均性能，顯著超越了知名基準。<lb/>更廣泛地說，這種概率記憶產生了可觀的增益，並探索了在部分可觀察環境中代理記憶的新方向。

##### **Locality-aware Private Class Identification for Domain Adaptation with Extreme Label Shift**
2605.05567v1 by Chuan-Xian Ren, Cheng-Jun Guo, Hong Yan

Domain adaptation aims to transfer knowledge from a labeled source domain to an unlabeled target domain with different distributions. In real-world scenarios, the label spaces of the two domains often have an inclusion relationship, where some classes exist only in one domain but not the other. These non-overlapping classes are referred to as private classes. Identifying private class samples and mitigating their adverse effects is critical in the literature. Existing methods rely on the assumption that shifts in private classes are large enough to be considered outliers. However, the variance within a single shared class can be significantly larger than the difference between a private class and another shared class, challenging this assumption. Consequently, private classes substantially increase the difficulty of cross-domain classification. To address these issues, based on local transportation and metric properties of optimal transport (OT), a locality-aware private class identification approach is proposed in the form of a score function on transport mass. The effectiveness of the proposed approach is theoretically proven, highlighting the score function's strong ability to distinguish between shared and private class samples. Building on this, we introduce a reliable OT-based method (ReOT) for domain adaptation under severe label shift. ReOT minimizes classification risk while learning the separated cluster structure between the identified shared classes and private classes, effectively avoiding mismatch between shared-private sample pairs, thus ensuring that important knowledge is reliably transported intra-class to mitigate class-conditional discrepancy. Furthermore, a generalization upper bound of the target risk is provided for extreme label shift scenarios, which can be minimized by ReOT. Extensive experiments on benchmarks validate the effectiveness of ReOT.

摘要：領域適應旨在將知識從標記的源領域轉移到具有不同分佈的未標記目標領域。在現實場景中，兩個領域的標籤空間通常存在包含關係，其中某些類別僅存在於一個領域而不在另一個領域。這些不重疊的類別被稱為私有類別。在文獻中，識別私有類別樣本並減輕其不利影響至關重要。現有的方法依賴於私有類別的變化足夠大以被視為異常值的假設。然而，單一共享類別內的變異性可能顯著大於私有類別與另一共享類別之間的差異，這挑戰了這一假設。因此，私有類別大大增加了跨領域分類的難度。為了解決這些問題，基於局部傳輸和最優傳輸（OT）的度量特性，提出了一種基於局部性的私有類別識別方法，該方法以傳輸質量的分數函數形式呈現。所提出方法的有效性在理論上得到了證明，突顯了分數函數在區分共享和私有類別樣本方面的強大能力。在此基礎上，我們引入了一種可靠的基於OT的方法（ReOT），用於在嚴重標籤轉移下的領域適應。ReOT在學習識別的共享類別和私有類別之間的分離聚類結構的同時，最小化分類風險，有效避免共享-私有樣本對之間的錯配，從而確保重要知識在類內可靠地傳輸，以減輕類條件差異。此外，針對極端標籤轉移場景，提供了目標風險的一般化上界，該上界可以通過ReOT最小化。在基準上的大量實驗驗證了ReOT的有效性。

##### **SPARK: Self-Play with Asymmetric Reward from Knowledge Graphs**
2605.05546v1 by Hyobin Park, Taeseop Kim, Dong-Geol Choi

Self-play reinforcement learning has shown strong performance in domains with formally verifiable structure, such as mathematics and coding, where both problem generation and reward computation can be grounded in explicit rules. Extending this paradigm to scientific literature is more challenging: the relationships among multi-modal elements within and across documents are rarely made explicit in text, which makes automatic generation of relational reasoning questions difficult and weakens the reliability of reward signals. We propose SPARK (Self-Play with Asymmetric Reward from Knowledge Graphs), a framework that automatically constructs a unified knowledge graph (KG) from multi-document scientific literature and uses it as the structural basis for self-play. KG paths over multimodal nodes serve as a source for generating relational reasoning questions, and structured facts stored in the KG provide a basis for verifiable reward computation. A single small vision-language model (sVLM) alternates between Proposer and Solver roles under information asymmetry against a fixed KG, a design that we believe can be naturally extended toward online adaptation in future work. We evaluate SPARK on public benchmarks and a self-constructed cross-document multi-hop QA dataset. Results show that SPARK consistently outperforms flat-corpus-based self-play baselines, and the performance gap widens as hop count increases, suggesting that KG-structure grounding contributes to relational multi-hop reasoning beyond what unstructured corpus grounding can provide.

摘要：自我對弈強化學習在具有正式可驗證結構的領域（如數學和編程）中表現出色，因為這些領域的問題生成和獎勵計算都可以基於明確的規則。將這一範式擴展到科學文獻中則更具挑戰性：文檔內部及跨文檔的多模態元素之間的關係在文本中很少明確表達，這使得自動生成關係推理問題變得困難，並削弱了獎勵信號的可靠性。我們提出了SPARK（來自知識圖的自我對弈不對稱獎勵），這是一個自動構建統一知識圖（KG）的框架，該知識圖來自多文檔科學文獻，並用作自我對弈的結構基礎。KG在多模態節點上的路徑作為生成關係推理問題的來源，而存儲在KG中的結構化事實則為可驗證的獎勵計算提供基礎。一個小型視覺語言模型（sVLM）在固定KG下交替擔任提議者和解決者角色，這種設計我們相信可以自然地擴展到未來工作的在線適應。我們在公共基準和自建的跨文檔多跳問答數據集上評估SPARK。結果顯示，SPARK始終優於基於平面語料的自我對弈基準，並且隨著跳數增加，性能差距擴大，這表明KG結構的基礎有助於超越非結構語料基礎的關係多跳推理。

##### **AgenticRAG: Agentic Retrieval for Enterprise Knowledge Bases**
2605.05538v1 by Susheel Suresh, Hazel Mak, Shangpo Chou, Fred Kroon, Sahil Bhatnagar

We present AgenticRAG, a practical agentic harness for retrieval and analysis over enterprise knowledge bases. Standard RAG pipelines place significant burden of grounding on the search stack, constraining the language model to a fixed candidate set chosen deep in the retrieval process. Our approach reduces this overdependence by layering a lightweight harness on top of existing enterprise search infrastructure, equipping a reasoning LLM with search, find, open, and summarize tools enabling the model to iteratively retrieve information, navigate within documents, and analyze evidence autonomously. On three open benchmarks we observe substantial gains: $49.6\%$ recall@1 on BRIGHT (+21.8 pp over the best embedding baseline), 0.96 factuality on WixQA ($+13\%$ relative improvement), and $92\%$ answer correctness on FinanceBench--within 2 pp of oracle access to true evidence. Ablation studies show that the most significant factor is the shift from single-shot retrieval to agentic tool use ($5.9\times$ improvement), while multi-query search and in-document navigation contribute to both quality and efficiency. We present various design choices in our agentic harness that were informed by pre-production deployments. Our results demonstrate its suitability for real-world enterprise production environments.

摘要：我們提出了AgenticRAG，一種實用的代理式工具，用於檢索和分析企業知識庫。標準的RAG管道將大量的基礎工作負擔放在搜索堆疊上，限制了語言模型只能選擇在檢索過程中深度選擇的固定候選集。我們的方法通過在現有企業搜索基礎設施之上層疊一個輕量級的工具，減少了對這種過度依賴，為推理LLM配備了搜索、查找、打開和總結工具，使模型能夠迭代地檢索信息、在文檔中導航並自主分析證據。在三個開放基準上，我們觀察到顯著的增益：在BRIGHT上達到$49.6\%$的recall@1（比最佳嵌入基線提高了21.8個百分點），在WixQA上達到0.96的事實性（相對改善13%），在FinanceBench上達到$92\%$的答案正確率——與對真實證據的預言訪問僅相差2個百分點。消融研究顯示，最重要的因素是從單次檢索轉變為代理工具的使用（改善了$5.9\times$），而多查詢搜索和文檔內導航對質量和效率都有貢獻。我們展示了在我們的代理式工具中做出的各種設計選擇，這些選擇是基於預生產部署的啟發。我們的結果證明了其在現實世界企業生產環境中的適用性。

##### **LANTERN: LLM-Augmented Neurosymbolic Transfer with Experience-Gated Reasoning Networks**
2605.05478v1 by Mahyar Alinejad, Yue Wang, Amrit Singh Bedi, George Atia

Transfer learning in reinforcement learning (RL) seeks to accelerate learning in new tasks by leveraging knowledge from related sources. Existing neurosymbolic transfer methods, however, typically rely on manually specified task automata, assume a single source task, and use fixed knowledge-integration mechanisms that cannot adapt to varying source relevance. We propose LANTERN, a unified framework for multi-source neurosymbolic transfer that addresses these limitations through three components: (i) deterministic finite automata generated from natural language task descriptions using large language models, (ii) semantic embedding-based aggregation of multiple source policies weighted by cross-task similarity, and (iii) adaptive teacher-student gating based on temporal-difference error and semantic uncertainty. Across domains spanning resource management, navigation, and control, LANTERN achieves 40-60% improvements in sample efficiency over existing baselines while remaining robust to poorly aligned sources. These results demonstrate that multi-source, adaptively weighted neurosymbolic transfer can improve scalability and robustness in symbolic RL settings.

摘要：轉移學習在強化學習 (RL) 中旨在通過利用相關來源的知識來加速新任務的學習。 然而，現有的神經符號轉移方法通常依賴於手動指定的任務自動機，假設單一來源任務，並使用固定的知識整合機制，無法適應不同來源的重要性。 我們提出了 LANTERN，一個統一的多來源神經符號轉移框架，通過三個組件來解決這些限制：(i) 使用大型語言模型從自然語言任務描述生成的確定性有限自動機，(ii) 基於語義嵌入的多來源策略聚合，根據跨任務相似性加權，以及 (iii) 基於時間差錯和語義不確定性的自適應教師-學生閘控。 在資源管理、導航和控制等多個領域中， LANTERN 在樣本效率上比現有基準提高了 40-60%，同時對於不良對齊的來源保持穩健。 這些結果表明，多來源、自適應加權的神經符號轉移可以提高符號 RL 環境中的可擴展性和穩健性。

##### **A Unified Benchmark for Evaluating Knowledge Graph Construction Methods and Graph Neural Networks**
2605.05476v1 by Othmane Kabal, Mounira Harzallah, Fabrice Guillet, Hideaki Takeda, Ryutaro Ichise

Knowledge graphs automatically constructed from text are increasingly used in real-world applications. However, their inherent noise, fragmentation, and semantic inconsistencies significantly affect the performance of Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) on downstream tasks. Assessing their performance and robustness remains difficult, as it is often unclear whether observed results stem from the learning model or from the quality of the constructed graph itself. In this work, we introduce a dual-purpose benchmark designed to jointly evaluate (i) the performance of GNNs on noisy, text-derived graphs and (ii) the effectiveness of graph construction methods on a downstream task. The benchmark is built in the biomedical domain from a single textual corpus and includes two automatically constructed graphs generated using different extraction methods, alongside a high-quality reference graph curated by experts that serves as an upper performance bound. This design enables controlled comparison of construction methods and systematic evaluation of GNN robustness through semi-supervised node classification. We further provide a standardized, reproducible, and extensible evaluation framework, facilitating the integration of new graph extraction methods and learning models.

##### **Robustness of Graph Self-Supervised Learning to Real-World Noise: A Case Study on Text-Driven Biomedical Graphs**
2605.05463v1 by Othmane Kabal, Mounira Harzallah, Fabrice Guillet, Hideaki Takeda, Ryutaro Ichise

Graph Self-Supervised Learning (GSSL) offers a powerful paradigm for learning graph representations without labeled data. However, existing work assumes clean, manually curated graphs. Recent advances in NLP enable the large-scale automatic extraction of knowledge graphs from text, opening new opportunities for GSSL while introducing substantial real-world noise. This type of noise remains largely unexplored, as prior robustness studies typically rely on synthetic perturbations. To address this gap, we present the first comprehensive evaluation of GSSL methods on text-driven graphs for unsupervised term typing. We introduce Noise-Aware Text-Driven Graph GSSL (NATD-GSSL), a unified framework that combines automatic graph construction, graph refinement, and GSSL. Our evaluation follows a dual-graph protocol that contrasts a noisy graph derived from MedMentions with a clean Unified Medical Language System (UMLS) reference graph, aligned through a shared gold standard. Our results reveal variability in robustness across both pretext tasks and Graph Neural Network (GNN) architectures. Relation reconstruction is highly sensitive to noise and benefits from well-defined schemas, whereas feature reconstruction is considerably more robust, achieving performance comparable to clean-graph settings. Contrastive objectives are generally less affected by noise but depend strongly on alignment with downstream tasks. GNN architecture also plays a critical role: bidirectional relational message-passing designs are better suited to noisy, text-driven graphs, while unidirectional relational ones perform best on clean graphs. Overall, NATD-GSSL provides practical guidance for applying GSSL to real-world, noisy graphs and achieves up to a 7\% improvement over pretrained language model baselines. All code and benchmarks are publicly available at https://github.com/OthmaneKabal/MC2GAE.

摘要：圖形自監督學習（GSSL）提供了一種強大的範式，用於在沒有標記數據的情況下學習圖形表示。<lb/>然而，現有的研究假設圖形是乾淨且手動整理的。<lb/>近期在自然語言處理（NLP）方面的進展使得從文本中自動提取知識圖的規模化成為可能，這為GSSL開辟了新的機會，同時引入了大量的現實世界噪聲。<lb/>這種類型的噪聲仍然在很大程度上未被探索，因為之前的穩健性研究通常依賴於合成擾動。<lb/>為了解決這一空白，我們首次對基於文本的圖形進行了GSSL方法的綜合評估，以進行無監督的術語類型標記。<lb/>我們引入了噪聲感知文本驅動圖GSSL（NATD-GSSL），這是一個統一框架，結合了自動圖構建、圖精煉和GSSL。<lb/>我們的評估遵循雙圖協議，對比了從MedMentions衍生的噪聲圖與通過共享金標準對齊的乾淨統一醫學語言系統（UMLS）參考圖。<lb/>我們的結果顯示，在預訓練任務和圖神經網絡（GNN）架構之間的穩健性存在變異性。<lb/>關係重建對噪聲高度敏感，並從明確的模式中受益，而特徵重建則顯著更具穩健性，實現了與乾淨圖設置相當的性能。<lb/>對比目標通常不太受噪聲影響，但強烈依賴於與下游任務的對齊。<lb/>GNN架構也發揮了關鍵作用：雙向關係消息傳遞設計更適合於噪聲的文本驅動圖，而單向關係的設計在乾淨圖上表現最佳。<lb/>總體而言，NATD-GSSL為將GSSL應用於現實世界的噪聲圖提供了實用指導，並實現了比預訓練語言模型基準高出7%的改進。<lb/>所有代碼和基準測試均可在https://github.com/OthmaneKabal/MC2GAE上公開獲取。

##### **Authorization Propagation in Multi-Agent AI Systems: Identity Governance as Infrastructure**
2605.05440v1 by Krti Tallam

The security discussion around agentic AI focuses heavily on prompt injection. This paper argues that multi-agent systems also create a distinct authorization problem: maintaining authorization invariants as non-human principals retrieve data, delegate tasks, and synthesize results across changing boundaries. We call this problem authorization propagation. It is not reducible to prompt injection and is not fully addressed by classical access-control models such as RBAC, ABAC, or ReBAC. The paper formalizes authorization propagation as a workflow-level property, identifies three sub-problems (transitive delegation, aggregation inference, and temporal validity), and derives seven structural requirements for authorization architectures in multi-agent AI systems. Recent work on invocation-bound capability tokens, task-scoped authorization envelopes, dependency-graph policy enforcement, and execution-count revocation demonstrates that the field is converging on the problem, but not yet on a complete architecture. The central claim is that identity governance must be treated as infrastructure: evaluated continuously, enforced at every interaction boundary, and designed into the system before orchestration logic is allowed to scale. Preliminary implementation evidence from a production enterprise AI platform shows that ordinary system behavior, not only adversarial action, already produces the failures this model predicts.

摘要：安全討論圍繞著代理型人工智慧，重點集中在提示注入上。本文主張，多代理系統還產生了一個獨特的授權問題：在非人類主體檢索數據、委派任務並在變化的邊界之間綜合結果時，維持授權不變。我們稱這個問題為授權傳播。它無法簡化為提示注入，也未被傳統的訪問控制模型如RBAC、ABAC或ReBAC完全解決。本文將授權傳播形式化為工作流程層級的屬性，識別出三個子問題（傳遞委派、聚合推理和時間有效性），並推導出多代理AI系統中授權架構的七個結構要求。最近關於調用限制能力令牌、任務範圍授權信封、依賴圖政策執行和執行計數撤銷的研究表明，該領域正在朝著這個問題收斂，但尚未形成完整的架構。核心主張是身份治理必須被視為基礎設施：持續評估、在每個互動邊界強制執行，並在允許編排邏輯擴展之前設計進系統。來自一個生產企業AI平台的初步實施證據顯示，普通系統行為，而不僅僅是對抗行動，已經產生了這個模型所預測的失敗。

##### **On Semantic Loss Fine-Tuning Approach for Preventing Model Collapse in Causal Reasoning**
2605.05438v1 by Pratik Deshmukh, Atirek Gupta

Standard fine-tuning of transformer models on causal reasoning tasks leads to catastrophic model collapse, where models learn trivial solutions such as always predicting "Yes" or "No" regardless of input structure. We demonstrate that fine-tuning Gemma 270M on transitivity and d-separation tasks without semantic loss results in 100% collapse rate, with models achieving misleadingly high accuracy (73.9%) while learning no causal reasoning. We propose a semantic loss function with graph-based logical constraints and dynamic lambda scheduling that prevents this collapse. Our approach achieves 70.4% accuracy on transitivity tasks and 68.6% on d-separation tasks with stable, context-dependent predictions, representing a 42.7% improvement over collapsed baselines. Adversarial evaluation on 1,000 structural reasoning samples shows semantic models achieve 67-70% accuracy while collapsed models fail catastrophically at 43-71%. We validate our findings through comprehensive benchmarking on 200,000+ evaluation samples across five model variants, demonstrating that semantic loss is essential and not optional, for stable causal reasoning in transformers.

摘要：標準的微調Transformer模型在因果推理任務上會導致災難性的模型崩潰，模型學會了平凡的解決方案，例如無論輸入結構如何，總是預測「是」或「否」。我們展示了在不損失語義的情況下，對Gemma 270M進行微調以處理傳遞性和d-分離任務會導致100%的崩潰率，模型在學習不到因果推理的情況下，卻達到了誤導性的高準確率（73.9%）。我們提出了一種具有基於圖的邏輯約束和動態lambda調度的語義損失函數，防止這種崩潰。我們的方法在傳遞性任務上達到了70.4%的準確率，在d-分離任務上達到了68.6%的準確率，並且預測穩定且依賴於上下文，這比崩潰的基準提高了42.7%。在1,000個結構推理樣本上的對抗性評估顯示，語義模型的準確率達到67-70%，而崩潰模型的準確率卻在43-71%之間災難性失敗。我們通過對五種模型變體在200,000+評估樣本上的全面基準測試來驗證我們的發現，證明語義損失對於Transformer中的穩定因果推理是必不可少的，而不是可選的。

##### **Mise en Place for Agentic Coding: Deliberate Preparation as Context Engineering Methodology**
2605.05400v1 by Andrew Zigler

The rapid adoption of AI coding agents has produced a dominant workflow pattern -- often called "vibe coding" -- that prioritizes speed of implementation over deliberate preparation. We argue that this approach creates a systematic alignment problem: agents that lack sufficient context produce code requiring extensive debugging and refactoring, consuming substantial development time. Drawing on the culinary concept of mise en place (everything in its place; abbreviated MEP), we propose a three-phase preparation methodology for agentic coding: (1) contextual grounding, where domain expertise and tacit knowledge are externalized into structured documents; (2) collaborative specification, where human-agent dialogue produces detailed design artifacts; and (3) task decomposition, where specifications are converted into structured, dependency-aware task records. We report on the application of MEP during a competitive hackathon, where roughly two hours of preparation enabled a rapid parallel implementation of a full-stack educational platform by concurrent AI agents. We introduce the concept of context fluency as an emerging developer skill -- the ability to create rich, structured context that agents can act on -- and connect it to established frameworks in backward design and tacit knowledge externalization. We conclude with a research agenda for empirically validating preparation-phase methodologies in AI-assisted software development.

摘要：快速採用 AI 編碼代理已產生一種主導的工作流程模式——通常稱為「氛圍編碼」——該模式優先考慮實施速度而非深思熟慮的準備。 我們認為這種方法創造了一個系統性的對齊問題：缺乏足夠上下文的代理生成的代碼需要大量的調試和重構，消耗了大量的開發時間。 我們借鑒烹飪概念「mise en place」（一切就位；簡稱 MEP），提出了一種三階段的準備方法論以進行代理編碼： (1) 上下文基礎，將領域專業知識和隱性知識外部化為結構化文檔； (2) 協作規範，通過人類與代理的對話生成詳細的設計工件； (3) 任務分解，將規範轉化為結構化的、依賴感知的任務記錄。 我們報告了在一場競爭性黑客馬拉松中應用 MEP 的情況，在這場活動中，大約兩小時的準備使得多個 AI 代理能夠快速並行實施一個全棧教育平台。 我們引入了上下文流暢性作為一種新興的開發者技能——創建豐富、結構化的上下文，使代理能夠採取行動的能力——並將其與反向設計和隱性知識外部化的既有框架相連接。 我們以一個研究議程作結，旨在實證驗證 AI 輔助軟體開發中的準備階段方法論。

##### **How Far Are VLMs from Privacy Awareness in the Physical World? An Empirical Study**
2605.05340v1 by Junran Wang, Xinjie Shen, Zehao Jin, Pan Li

As Vision-Language Models (VLMs) are increasingly deployed as autonomous cognitive cores for embodied assistants, evaluating their privacy awareness in physical environments becomes critical. Unlike digital chatbots, these agents operate in intimate spaces, such as homes and hospitals, where they possess the physical agency to observe and manipulate privacy-sensitive information and artifacts. However, current benchmarks remain limited to unimodal, text-based representations that cannot capture the demands of real-world settings. To bridge this gap, we present ImmersedPrivacy, an interactive audio-visual evaluation framework that simulates realistic physical environments using a Unity-based simulator. ImmersedPrivacy evaluates physically grounded privacy awareness across three progressive tiers that test a model's ability to identify sensitive items in cluttered scenes, adapt to shifting social contexts, and resolve conflicts between explicit commands and inferred privacy constraints. Our evaluation of 12 state-of-the-art models reveals consistent deficits. In cluttered scenes, all models exhibit monotonic performance decay as scene complexity grows due to perceptual deficit. When social context shifts, no model exceed 65% selection accuracy. Under conflicting commands, the best model gemini-3.1-pro perfectly balances task completion and privacy preservation in only 51% of cases. These findings reveal that current VLMs in the physical world suffer from perceptual fragility and fail to let their knowledge of privacy cues govern their situated behavior. Our code and data is available at https://github.com/immersed-privacy/immersed-privacy .

摘要：隨著視覺-語言模型（VLMs）越來越多地被部署為具身助手的自主認知核心，評估它們在物理環境中的隱私意識變得至關重要。與數位聊天機器人不同，這些代理在親密空間中運作，例如家庭和醫院，在這些地方它們擁有觀察和操控隱私敏感信息和物品的實體能力。然而，目前的基準仍然僅限於單一模態的文本表示，無法捕捉現實世界環境的需求。為了彌補這一差距，我們提出了ImmersedPrivacy，一個互動式音視覺評估框架，使用基於Unity的模擬器來模擬現實的物理環境。ImmersedPrivacy在三個進階層次上評估物理基礎的隱私意識，測試模型識別雜亂場景中敏感物品的能力、適應變化的社交背景以及解決明確命令和推斷的隱私限制之間的衝突。我們對12個最先進模型的評估顯示出一致的不足。在雜亂的場景中，所有模型的性能隨著場景複雜性的增加而單調下降，這是由於感知缺陷造成的。當社交背景發生變化時，沒有模型的選擇準確率超過65%。在衝突命令下，最佳模型gemini-3.1-pro在僅51%的情況下完美平衡任務完成和隱私保護。這些發現揭示了當前VLMs在物理世界中存在感知脆弱性，未能讓它們對隱私線索的知識支配其具體行為。我們的代碼和數據可在https://github.com/immersed-privacy/immersed-privacy獲得。

##### **MRI-Eval: A Tiered Benchmark for Evaluating LLM Performance on MRI Physics and GE Scanner Operations Knowledge**
2605.05175v1 by Perry E. Radau

Background: Existing MRI LLM benchmarks rely mainly on review-book multiple-choice questions, where top proprietary models already score highly, limiting discrimination. No systematic benchmark has evaluated vendor-specific scanner operational knowledge central to research MRI practice. Purpose: We developed MRI-Eval, a tiered benchmark for relative model comparison on MRI physics and GE scanner operations knowledge using primary multiple-choice questions (MCQ), with stem-only and primed diagnostic conditions as complementary analyses. Methods: MRI-Eval includes 1365 scored items across nine categories and three difficulty tiers from textbooks, GE scanner manuals, programming course materials, and expert-generated questions. Five model families were evaluated (GPT-5.4, Claude Opus 4.6, Claude Sonnet 4.6, Gemini 2.5 Pro, Llama 3.3 70B). MCQ was primary; stem-only removed options and used an independent LLM judge; primed stem-only tested responses to incorrect user claims. Results: Overall MCQ accuracy was 93.2% to 97.1%. GE scanner operations was the lowest category for every model (88.2% to 94.6%). In stem-only, frontier-model accuracy fell to 58.4% to 61.1%, and Llama 3.3 70B fell to 37.1%; GE scanner operations stem-only accuracy was 13.8% to 29.8%. Conclusion: High MCQ performance can mask weak free-text recall, especially for vendor-specific operational knowledge. MRI-Eval is most informative as a relative comparison benchmark rather than an absolute competency measure and supports caution in using raw LLM outputs for GE-specific protocol guidance.

摘要：背景：現有的 MRI LLM 基準主要依賴於回顧書籍的多選題，而頂尖的專有模型已經取得了高分，這限制了區分度。尚未有系統性的基準評估與研究 MRI 實踐相關的供應商特定掃描器操作知識。目的：我們開發了 MRI-Eval，這是一個分層基準，用於相對模型比較 MRI 物理學和 GE 掃描器操作知識，使用主要的多選題（MCQ），並以僅題幹和啟發式診斷條件作為補充分析。方法：MRI-Eval 包括來自教科書、GE 掃描器手冊、編程課程材料和專家生成問題的 1365 個評分項目，涵蓋九個類別和三個難度層級。評估了五個模型系列（GPT-5.4、Claude Opus 4.6、Claude Sonnet 4.6、Gemini 2.5 Pro、Llama 3.3 70B）。MCQ 是主要的；僅題幹移除了選項並使用獨立的 LLM 評判；啟發式僅題幹測試對不正確用戶聲明的回應。結果：整體 MCQ 準確率為 93.2% 到 97.1%。GE 掃描器操作是每個模型中最低的類別（88.2% 到 94.6%）。在僅題幹中，前沿模型的準確率降至 58.4% 到 61.1%，而 Llama 3.3 70B 降至 37.1%；GE 掃描器操作的僅題幹準確率為 13.8% 到 29.8%。結論：高 MCQ 表現可能掩蓋了較弱的自由文本回憶，尤其是對供應商特定操作知識的回憶。MRI-Eval 作為相對比較基準比作為絕對能力測量更具信息性，並支持在使用原始 LLM 輸出進行 GE 特定協議指導時保持謹慎。

##### **Joint Treatment Effect Estimation from Incomplete Healthcare Data: Temporal Causal Normalizing Flows with LLM-driven Evolutionary MNAR Imputation**
2605.05125v1 by Olivia Jullian Parra, Sara Zoccheddu, David Catalan Cerezo, Tom Forzy, Franziska Ulrich, William Sutcliffe, Jakob Martin Burgstaller, Oliver Senn, Patrick Owen, Nicola Serra

Target trial emulation (TTE) enables causal questions to be studied with observational data when randomized controlled trials (RCTs) are infeasible. Yet treatment-effect methods often address causal estimation, missingness, and temporal structure separately, limiting their robustness in electronic health records (EHRs), where time-varying confounding and missing-not-at-random (MNAR) biomarkers can reach 50%--80%. We propose a two-stage pipeline for treatment effect estimation from incomplete longitudinal EHRs. First, CausalFlow-T, a directed acyclic graph (DAG)-constrained normalizing flow with long short-term memory (LSTM)-encoded patient history, performs exact invertible counterfactual inference, avoiding approximation errors from variational inference and separating confounding through explicit causal structure. Ablations on four synthetic and one semi-synthetic benchmark with known counterfactuals show that DAG constraints and exact inference address distinct failure modes: neither compensates for the other. Second, because CausalFlow-T requires completed inputs, we introduce an LLM-driven evolutionary imputer that proposes executable imputation operators rather than individual entries, and evaluate it with three large language model (LLM) backends, including two open-source models. Across 30%--80% MNAR missingness, this imputer achieves the best pooled rank over biomarker and causal metrics, leading in point-wise accuracy and temporal extrapolation while preserving average treatment effect (ATE) recovery as statistical baselines degrade. On Swiss primary-care EHRs from adults with type 2 diabetes initiating a GLP-1 receptor agonist or SGLT-2 inhibitor, the pipeline estimates a per-protocol weight-loss difference of -0.98 kg [95% CI -1.01, -0.96] favoring GLP-1 receptor agonists, consistent with randomized evidence and obtained from realistically incomplete real-world EHRs.

摘要：目標試驗模擬（TTE）使得在隨機對照試驗（RCT）不可行的情況下，可以利用觀察數據研究因果問題。<lb/>然而，治療效果方法通常將因果估計、缺失性和時間結構分開處理，這限制了它們在電子健康記錄（EHRs）中的穩健性，因為時間變化的混雜因素和隨機缺失（MNAR）生物標記的缺失率可能達到50%至80%。<lb/>我們提出了一個兩階段的管道，用於從不完整的縱向EHR中估計治療效果。<lb/>首先，CausalFlow-T是一種受限於有向無循環圖（DAG）的正規化流，結合長短期記憶（LSTM）編碼的病人歷史，進行精確的可逆反事實推斷，避免了變分推斷中的近似誤差，並通過明確的因果結構分離混雜因素。<lb/>在四個合成基準和一個半合成基準上進行的消融實驗顯示，DAG約束和精確推斷解決了不同的失敗模式：彼此之間並不互相補償。<lb/>其次，由於CausalFlow-T需要完整的輸入，我們引入了一種由大型語言模型（LLM）驅動的進化插補器，該插補器提出可執行的插補操作符，而不是單獨的條目，並使用三個大型語言模型後端進行評估，包括兩個開源模型。<lb/>在30%至80%的MNAR缺失率下，這個插補器在生物標記和因果指標上達到了最佳的綜合排名，在逐點準確性和時間外推方面領先，同時在統計基準下降的情況下保持平均治療效果（ATE）的恢復。<lb/>在瑞士的初級保健EHR中，針對接受GLP-1受體激動劑或SGLT-2抑制劑的2型糖尿病成人，該管道估計的每個協議體重減輕差異為-0.98公斤 [95% CI -1.01, -0.96]，支持GLP-1受體激動劑，與隨機證據一致，並且是從現實中不完整的真實世界EHR中獲得的。

##### **Continual Knowledge Updating in LLM Systems: Learning Through Multi-Timescale Memory Dynamics**
2605.05097v2 by Andreas Pattichis, Constantine Dovrolis

LLMs are trained once, then deployed into a world that never stops changing. External memory compensates for this, but most systems manage it explicitly rather than letting it adapt on its own. Biological memory works differently: coupled multi-timescale dynamics make new associations immediately usable, strengthen what repetition confirms, and let the rest fade. We argue that external memory should follow a similar principle. In Memini, this view takes the form of an associative memory that organizes knowledge as a directed graph. Each edge carries two coupled internal variables, one fast and one slow, following the Benna-Fusi model of synaptic consolidation. From this coupling, episodic sensitivity, gradual consolidation, and selective forgetting emerge as facets of a single mechanism, reframing external memory as a learning substrate that reorganizes through its own dynamics.

摘要：LLMs 只訓練一次，然後被部署到一個不斷變化的世界中。外部記憶彌補了這一點，但大多數系統是明確管理的，而不是讓它自行適應。生物記憶的運作方式不同：耦合的多時間尺度動態使新的聯結立即可用，強化重複所確認的內容，並讓其餘的逐漸消退。我們主張外部記憶應遵循類似的原則。在 Memini 中，這一觀點以一種將知識組織為有向圖的聯想記憶形式呈現。每條邊都承載著兩個耦合的內部變數，一個快，另一個慢，遵循 Benna-Fusi 突觸鞏固模型。從這種耦合中，情節敏感性、逐漸鞏固和選擇性遺忘作為單一機制的不同面向出現，將外部記憶重新框架為一種通過自身動態重新組織的學習基質。

##### **Automatically Finding and Validating Unexpected Side-Effects of Interventions on Language Models**
2605.05090v1 by Quintin Pope, Ajay Hayagreeve Balaji, Jacques Thibodeau, Xiaoli Fern

We present an automated, contrastive evaluation pipeline for auditing the behavioral impact of interventions on large language models. Given a base model $M_1$ and an intervention model $M_2$, our method compares their free-form, multi-token generations across aligned prompt contexts and produces human-readable, statistically validated natural-language hypotheses describing how the models differ, along with recurring themes that summarize patterns across validated hypotheses.
  We evaluate the approach in synthetic setting by injecting known behavioral changes and showing that the pipeline reliably recovers them. We then apply it to three real-world interventions, reasoning distillation, knowledge editing and unlearning, demonstrating that the method surfaces both intended and unexpected behavioral shifts, distinguishes large from subtle interventions, and does not hallucinate differences when effects are absent or misaligned with the prompt bank. Overall, the pipeline provides a statistically grounded and interpretable tool for post-hoc auditing of intervention-induced changes in model behavior.

摘要：我們提出了一個自動化的對比評估流程，用於審核干預措施對大型語言模型的行為影響。給定一個基礎模型 $M_1$ 和一個干預模型 $M_2$，我們的方法比較它們在對齊的提示上下文中自由形式的多標記生成，並產生可讀的、經過統計驗證的自然語言假設，描述模型之間的差異，以及總結經過驗證的假設中模式的重複主題。<lb/>我們在合成環境中評估該方法，通過注入已知的行為變化，顯示該流程可靠地恢復了這些變化。然後，我們將其應用於三個現實世界的干預措施，包括推理蒸餾、知識編輯和遺忘，展示該方法能夠揭示預期和意外的行為變化，區分大型和微妙的干預，並且在效果缺失或與提示庫不對齊時不會虛構差異。總的來說，該流程提供了一個統計基礎和可解釋的工具，用於事後審核干預引起的模型行為變化。

##### **Uno-Orchestra: Parsimonious Agent Routing via Selective Delegation**
2605.05007v1 by Zhiqing Cui, Haotong Xie, Jiahao Yuan, Cheng Yang, Hanqing Wang, Yuxin Wu, Yifan Wu, Siru Zhong, Tao Yu, Yifu Guo, Siyu Zhang, Xinlei Yu, Qibing Ren, Usman Naseem

Large language model (LLM) multi-agent systems typically rely on rigid orchestration, committing either to flat per-query routing or to hand-engineered task decomposition, so decomposition depth, worker choice, and inference budget are not jointly optimized under one objective. We introduce Uno-Orchestra, a unified orchestration policy that selectively decomposes a task and dispatches each subtask to an admissible (model, primitive) pair, with both decisions learned together from curated RL trajectories grounded in real worker interactions. Against 22 baselines on a 13-benchmark suite spanning math, code, knowledge, long-context, and agentic tool-use, Uno-Orchestra reaches 77.0% macro pass@1, roughly 16% above the strongest workflow baseline, at roughly an order of magnitude lower per-query cost, advancing the accuracy-efficiency frontier of selective delegation.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLM）多代理系統通常依賴於僵化的協調，承諾要麼是平坦的每查詢路由，要麼是手工設計的任務分解，因此分解深度、工作者選擇和推理預算並未在一個目標下共同優化。我們推出了Uno-Orchestra，一種統一的協調政策，選擇性地分解任務並將每個子任務派遣到一個可接受的（模型，原語）對，這兩個決策是從基於真實工作者互動的策劃強化學習軌跡中共同學習的。在涵蓋數學、代碼、知識、長上下文和代理工具使用的13個基準套件上，Uno-Orchestra在22個基準上達到了77.0%的宏觀通過率@1，這比最強的工作流程基準高出約16%，且每查詢成本低了大約一個量級，推進了選擇性委託的準確性-效率邊界。

##### **Why Expert Alignment Is Hard: Evidence from Subjective Evaluation**
2605.04972v1 by Tzu-Mi Lin, Wataru Hirota, Tatsuya Ishigaki, Lung-Hao Lee, Chung-Chi Chen

Aligning large language models with expert judgment is especially difficult in subjective evaluation tasks, where experts may disagree, rely on tacit criteria, and change their judgments over time. In this paper, we study expert alignment as a way to understand this difficulty. Using expert evaluations and follow-up questionnaires, we examine how different forms of expert information affect alignment and what this reveals about subjective judgment. Our findings show four consistent patterns. First, alignment difficulty varies substantially across experts, suggesting that expert evaluation styles differ widely in their distance from a model's prior behavior. Second, explicit criteria and reasoning do not always improve alignment, indicating that expert judgment is not fully captured by verbalized rules. Third, editing is sensitive to both the number and the identity of examples, with small numbers of edits providing useful but unstable gains. Fourth, alignment difficulty differs across evaluation dimensions: dimensions grounded more directly in proposal content are easier to align, while dimensions requiring external knowledge or value-based judgment remain harder. Taken together, these results suggest that expert alignment is difficult not only because of model limitations, but also because subjective evaluation is inherently heterogeneous, partly tacit, dimension-dependent, and temporally unstable.

摘要：將大型語言模型與專家判斷對齊在主觀評估任務中尤其困難，因為專家之間可能存在分歧，依賴於隱性標準，並且隨著時間的推移改變他們的判斷。<lb/>在本文中，我們研究專家對齊作為理解這一困難的一種方式。<lb/>通過專家評估和後續問卷調查，我們檢視不同形式的專家信息如何影響對齊，以及這揭示了什麼關於主觀判斷的內容。<lb/>我們的研究結果顯示出四種一致的模式。<lb/>首先，對齊的困難在不同專家之間有著顯著的變化，這表明專家的評估風格在其與模型先前行為的距離上存在廣泛的差異。<lb/>其次，明確的標準和推理並不總是能改善對齊，這表明專家判斷並未完全被口頭化的規則所捕捉。<lb/>第三，編輯對例子的數量和身份都很敏感，少量的編輯提供了有用但不穩定的增益。<lb/>第四，對齊的困難在評估維度上有所不同：更直接基於提案內容的維度更容易對齊，而需要外部知識或基於價值的判斷的維度則仍然較難。<lb/>綜合來看，這些結果表明，專家對齊的困難不僅僅是因為模型的局限性，還因為主觀評估本質上是異質的，部分是隱性的，依賴於維度，並且在時間上不穩定。

##### **Skill Neologisms: Towards Skill-based Continual Learning**
2605.04970v1 by Antonin Berthon, Nicolas Astorga, Mihaela van der Schaar

Modern LLMs show mastery over an ever-growing range of skills, as well as the ability to compose them flexibly. However, extending model capabilities to new skills in a scalable manner is an open-problem: fine-tuning and parameter-efficient variants risk catastrophic forgetting, while context-based approaches have limited expressiveness and are constrained by the model's effective context. We explore skill neologisms--i.e., soft tokens integrated in the model's vocabulary and optimized to improve capabilities over a specific skill--as a way to selectively extend model capabilities to new skills without weight updates. We first observe that off-the-shelf pre-trained LLMs already demonstrate tokens associated with procedural knowledge. We then show that skill neologisms can be learned to improve model capabilities on specific skills while being composable with out-of-distribution skills, and that independently trained skill neologisms can be composed zero-shot. These results suggest that skill neologisms may provide a scalable path towards skill-based continual learning.

摘要：現代的 LLM 展現了對不斷增長的技能範圍的掌握，以及靈活組合這些技能的能力。<lb/>然而，以可擴展的方式將模型能力擴展到新技能仍然是一個未解決的問題：微調和參數高效變體存在災難性遺忘的風險，而基於上下文的方法表達能力有限，並受到模型有效上下文的限制。<lb/>我們探索技能新詞——即集成在模型詞彙中的軟標記，並優化以提升特定技能的能力——作為選擇性擴展模型能力到新技能而不需要更新權重的一種方式。<lb/>我們首先觀察到現成的預訓練 LLM 已經展示了與程序性知識相關的標記。<lb/>然後，我們展示了技能新詞可以被學習以改善模型在特定技能上的能力，同時能與分佈外的技能進行組合，並且獨立訓練的技能新詞可以零樣本組合。<lb/>這些結果表明，技能新詞可能提供了一條可擴展的途徑，朝向基於技能的持續學習。

##### **Reliable Modeling of Distribution Shifts via Displacement-Reshaped Optimal Transport**
2605.04965v1 by Philip Naumann, Jacob Kauffmann, Klaus-Robert Müller, Grégoire Montavon

Optimal transport (OT) is a central framework for modeling distribution shifts. Because OT compares distributions directly in input space, a well-designed ground metric between observations is essential to ensure that the optimizer does not violate the true geometry of change. We propose Displacement-Reshaped Optimal Transport (ReshapeOT), a method that reshapes the ground metric by integrating observed sample displacements as an additional source of knowledge. Technically, ReshapeOT replaces the Euclidean metric with a Mahalanobis distance estimated from displacement second moments. This effectively carves expressways through the input space, inviting transport solutions that better align with observed displacements. Our method is computationally lightweight, integrates seamlessly into any OT solver that operates on a cost matrix, and can be kernelized for further flexibility. Experiments on synthetic and real-world data show that ReshapeOT achieves substantial gains in transport reliability. We further demonstrate our method's usefulness in two practical use cases.

摘要：最佳運輸（OT）是建模分佈變化的核心框架。由於 OT 直接在輸入空間中比較分佈，因此在觀察之間設計良好的基準度量是至關重要的，以確保優化器不會違反變化的真實幾何。 我們提出了位移重塑最佳運輸（ReshapeOT），這是一種通過將觀察到的樣本位移整合為額外的知識來源來重塑基準度量的方法。 從技術上講，ReshapeOT 用從位移二次矩估計的馬哈拉諾比斯距離替代歐幾里得度量。 這有效地在輸入空間中開鑿了快速通道，邀請更好地與觀察到的位移對齊的運輸解決方案。 我們的方法計算輕量級，無縫集成到任何在成本矩陣上運行的 OT 求解器中，並且可以進行核化以獲得進一步的靈活性。 在合成數據和現實世界數據上的實驗顯示，ReshapeOT 在運輸可靠性方面取得了顯著的增益。 我們進一步展示了我們方法在兩個實際用例中的有效性。

##### **Storage Is Not Memory: A Retrieval-Centered Architecture for Agent Recall**
2605.04897v1 by Joshua Adler, Guy Zehavi

Extraction at ingestion is the wrong primitive for agent memory: content discarded before the query is known cannot be recovered at retrieval time. We propose True Memory, a six-layer architecture that shifts the center of the system from a storage schema to a multi-stage retrieval pipeline operating over events preserved verbatim. The full system runs as a single SQLite file on commodity CPU with no external database, vector index, graph store, or GPU. On LoCoMo (1,540 questions across 10 multi-session conversations), True Memory Pro reaches 93.0% accuracy (3-run mean) against 61.4% for Mem0, 65.4% for Supermemory, approximately 71% for Zep, and 94.5% for EverMemOS under a matched gpt-4.1-mini answer model. On LongMemEval (500 questions), True Memory Pro reaches 87.8% (3-run mean). On BEAM-1M (700 questions at the 1-million-token scale), True Memory Pro reaches 76.6% (3-run mean), above the prior published result of 73.9% for Hindsight. A 56-configuration ablation shows a 1.3-percentage-point spread within the top-performing configuration family.

摘要：提取在攝取時是代理記憶的錯誤原始概念：在查詢已知之前被丟棄的內容無法在檢索時恢復。我們提出了真實記憶（True Memory），這是一個六層架構，將系統的中心從存儲模式轉移到一個多階段檢索管道，該管道對事件進行逐字保留。整個系統作為一個單一的SQLite文件運行在普通CPU上，無需外部數據庫、向量索引、圖形存儲或GPU。在LoCoMo（10個多會話對話中的1,540個問題）上，真實記憶專業版（True Memory Pro）達到93.0%的準確率（3次運行平均），而Mem0為61.4%，Supermemory為65.4%，Zep約為71%，EverMemOS在匹配的gpt-4.1-mini答案模型下為94.5%。在LongMemEval（500個問題）上，真實記憶專業版達到87.8%（3次運行平均）。在BEAM-1M（700個問題，規模為100萬個標記）上，真實記憶專業版達到76.6%（3次運行平均），高於Hindsight先前發表的73.9%的結果。一個56配置的消融實驗顯示在表現最佳的配置家族中有1.3個百分點的差距。

##### **Uncertainty-Aware Exploratory Direct Preference Optimization for Multimodal Large Language Models**
2605.04874v1 by Huatian Zhang, Zhendong Mao, Lei Zhang, Yongdong Zhang

Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) has proven to be an effective solution for mitigating hallucination in Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) by learning from preference pairs. One of its key challenges lies in how to transfer the sequence-level preference into fine-grained supervision on visual fidelity. To safeguard vision-related tokens that are prone to hallucination, existing methods typically allocate training emphasis according to the model's self-assessed visual sensitivity signals. However, such sensitivity, estimated by a model still under training, introduces self-referential bias: reinforcing already well-learned visual cues while neglecting hard-to-perceive but critical details, thereby limiting deeper alignment. In this work, we propose an Uncertainty-aware Exploratory Direct Preference Optimization (UE-DPO) method for MLLMs, which enables the model to uncover its cognitive deficiencies and actively explore for self-correction, guided by token-level epistemic uncertainty. Specifically, we first quantify the uncertainty from the model's failure to ground token predictions in the given image. Then, based on an uncertainty-aware exploration intensity, we encourage more learning pressure on visually deficient tokens in preferred samples, and alleviate the over-penalization of beneficial knowledge in dispreferred samples. Further, we provide a theoretical justification for our method, and extensive experiments demonstrate its effectiveness and robustness.

摘要：直接偏好優化（DPO）已被證明是一種有效的解決方案，可以通過從偏好對中學習來減輕多模態大型語言模型（MLLMs）中的幻覺問題。它的一個主要挑戰在於如何將序列級別的偏好轉化為對視覺真實性的細緻監督。為了保護易於產生幻覺的與視覺相關的標記，現有的方法通常根據模型自我評估的視覺敏感信號來分配訓練重點。然而，這種敏感性是由仍在訓練中的模型估算的，這引入了自我參照偏差：強化已經學得良好的視覺線索，同時忽略難以感知但至關重要的細節，從而限制了更深層次的對齊。在本研究中，我們提出了一種不確定性感知的探索性直接偏好優化（UE-DPO）方法，適用於 MLLMs，該方法使模型能夠發現其認知缺陷並主動探索以進行自我修正，並以標記級別的認知不確定性為指導。具體來說，我們首先量化模型在給定圖像中無法對標記預測進行基準的情況下的不確定性。然後，基於不確定性感知的探索強度，我們鼓勵在偏好的樣本中對視覺不足的標記施加更多的學習壓力，並減輕對不受偏好的樣本中有益知識的過度懲罰。此外，我們為我們的方法提供了理論依據，並通過大量實驗證明了其有效性和穩健性。

##### **Gyan: An Explainable Neuro-Symbolic Language Model**

Transformer based pre-trained large language models have become ubiquitous. Here, we describe Gyan, an explainable language model based on a novel non-transformer architecture, without any of these limitations. ##### **Knowledge-Free Correlated Agreement for Incentivizing Federated Learning**
